SCHEDULLER ::=
run_queue := [];
run_prior := -1;
run_now := "";
run_queue := push(run_queue, [[run_prior, run_now]]);
(
ready_pan_ctr_th_imp?prior -->
    if run_prior >= prior then
        run_queue := push(run_queue, [[prior, "pan_ctr_th_imp"]])
    else
        run_now == "img_acq_imp" -> busy_img_acq_imp!;
        run_now == "comp_obs_pos_imp" -> busy_comp_obs_pos_imp!;
        run_now == "comp_acc_imp" -> busy_comp_acc_imp!;
        run_now == "velo_voter_imp" -> busy_velo_voter_imp!;
        run_now := "pan_ctr_th_imp";
        run_prior := prior;
        run_pan_ctr_th_imp!
    endif
$
ready_img_acq_imp?prior -->
    if run_prior >= prior then
        run_queue := push(run_queue, [[prior, "img_acq_imp"]])
    else
        run_now == "pan_ctr_th_imp" -> busy_pan_ctr_th_imp!;
        run_now == "comp_obs_pos_imp" -> busy_comp_obs_pos_imp!;
        run_now == "comp_acc_imp" -> busy_comp_acc_imp!;
        run_now == "velo_voter_imp" -> busy_velo_voter_imp!;
        run_now := "img_acq_imp";
        run_prior := prior;
        run_img_acq_imp!
    endif
$
ready_comp_obs_pos_imp?prior -->
    if run_prior >= prior then
        run_queue := push(run_queue, [[prior, "comp_obs_pos_imp"]])
    else
        run_now == "img_acq_imp" -> busy_img_acq_imp!;
        run_now == "pan_ctr_th_imp" -> busy_pan_ctr_th_imp!;
        run_now == "comp_acc_imp" -> busy_comp_acc_imp!;
        run_now == "velo_voter_imp" -> busy_velo_voter_imp!;
        run_now := "comp_obs_pos_imp";
        run_prior := prior;
        run_comp_obs_pos_imp!
    endif
$
ready_comp_acc_imp?prior -->
    if run_prior >= prior then
        run_queue := push(run_queue, [[prior, "comp_acc_imp"]])
    else
        run_now == "img_acq_imp" -> busy_img_acq_imp!;
        run_now == "comp_obs_pos_imp" -> busy_comp_obs_pos_imp!;
        run_now == "pan_ctr_th_imp" -> busy_pan_ctr_th_imp!;
        run_now == "velo_voter_imp" -> busy_velo_voter_imp!;
        run_now := "comp_acc_imp";
        run_prior := prior;
        run_comp_acc_imp!
    endif
$
ready_velo_voter_imp?prior -->
    if run_prior >= prior then
        run_queue := push(run_queue, [[prior, "velo_voter_imp"]])
    else
        run_now == "img_acq_imp" -> busy_img_acq_imp!;
        run_now == "comp_obs_pos_imp" -> busy_comp_obs_pos_imp!;
        run_now == "comp_acc_imp" -> busy_comp_acc_imp!;
        run_now == "pan_ctr_th_imp" -> busy_pan_ctr_th_imp!;
        run_now := "velo_voter_imp";
        run_prior := prior;
        run_velo_voter_imp!
    endif
$
free?proc_name -->
    if proc_name == run_now then
        (run_prior, run_now) := get_max(run_queue);
        run_prior >= 0 -> run_queue := pop_max(run_queue);
        run_now == "pan_ctr_th_imp" -> run_pan_ctr_th_imp!;
        run_now == "img_acq_imp" -> run_img_acq_imp!;
        run_now == "comp_obs_pos_imp" -> run_comp_obs_pos_imp!;
        run_now == "velo_voter_imp" -> run_velo_voter_imp!
    else
        run_queue := del_proc(run_queue, proc_name)
    endif
)**

ACT_img_acq_imp ::=
(act_img_acq_imp!; wait(0.05))**

COM_img_acq_imp ::=
state := "inactive"; prior := 1;
(
if state == "inactive" then
    act_img_acq_imp?;
    t := 0; got_result := 0; state := "ready"
elif state == "ready" then
    ready_img_acq_imp!prior;
    <t_dot = 1 & t < 0.05> |> [] (run_img_acq_imp? --> state := "running");
    t == 0.05 -> (free!"img_acq_imp"; state := "inactive")
else  # state == "running"
    got_result == 0 ->
    (
        exe_time := 0;
        (
        tran_img2?image --> got_result := 1
        $
        busy_img_acq_imp? --> state := "ready"
        )
    );
    got_result == 1 ->
    (
        <t_dot = 1, exe_time_dot = 1 & exe_time < 0.04 && t < 0.05> |> [] (busy_img_acq_imp? --> state := "ready");
        if t == 0.05 then
            free!"img_acq_imp"; state := "inactive"
        elif exe_time >= 0.01 then
            tran_proc_img!image; free!"img_acq_imp"; state := "inactive"
        else  # t < 0.05 & exe_time < 0.01
            skip
        endif
    )
endif
)**

COM_comp_obs_pos_imp ::=
state := "inactive"; prior := 1;
(
if state == "inactive" then
    act_comp_obs_pos_imp?;
    t := 0; got_result := 0; state := "ready"
elif state == "ready" then
    ready_comp_obs_pos_imp!prior;
    <t_dot = 1 & t < 0.1> |> [] (run_comp_obs_pos_imp? --> state := "running");
    t == 0.1 -> (free!"comp_obs_pos_imp"; state := "inactive")
else  # state == "running"
    got_result == 0 ->
    (
        exe_time := 0;
        (
        tran_obs_pos_radar2?obs_pos_radar -->
            tran_proc_img1?proc_img;
            obs_pos_radar < 0 -> obs_pos_radar := 0;
            proc_img < 0 -> proc_img := 0;
            if obs_pos_radar == 0 then
                obs_pos := proc_img
            elif proc_img == 0 then
                obs_pos := obs_pos_radar
            else
                obs_pos := min(obs_pos_radar, proc_img)
            endif;
            got_result := 1
        $
        busy_comp_obs_pos_imp? --> state := "ready"
        )
    );
    got_result == 1 ->
    (
        <t_dot = 1, exe_time_dot = 1 & exe_time < 0.05 && t < 0.1> |> [] (busy_comp_obs_pos_imp? --> state := "ready");
        if t == 0.1 then
            free!"comp_obs_pos_imp"; state := "inactive"
        elif exe_time >= 0.02 then
            tran_obs_pos!obs_pos; free!"comp_obs_pos_imp"; state := "inactive"
        else  # t < 0.1 & exe_time < 0.02
            skip
        endif
    )
endif
)**

GLOBAL_TIME ::=
t := 0; (<t_dot = 1 & t < 20> |> [] (get_global_time!t --> skip))**

ACT_comp_acc_imp ::=
(act_comp_acc_imp!; wait(0.005))**

COM_comp_acc_imp ::=
total_error := 0; curr_error := 0;
last_time := 0;
K_P := 2.5; K_I := 1;
safe_d := 10;
saturation := 0;

state := "inactive"; prior := 2;
(
if state == "inactive" then
    act_comp_acc_imp?;
    t := 0; got_result := 0; state := "ready"
elif state == "ready" then
    ready_comp_acc_imp!prior;
    <t_dot = 1 & t < 0.005> |> [] (run_comp_acc_imp? --> state := "running");
    t == 0.005 -> (free!"comp_acc_imp"; state := "inactive")
else  # state == "running"
    got_result == 0 ->
    (
        exe_time := 0;
        (
        tran_des_v1?des_v -->
            tran_veh_v1?veh_v;
            tran_obs_pos1?obs_pos;
            tran_veh_pos2?veh_pos;
            get_global_time?curr_time;
            total_error := total_error + curr_error * (curr_time - last_time) * (1 - saturation);
            curr_error := des_v - veh_v;
            last_time := curr_time;
            des_a := K_P * curr_error + K_I * total_error;
            saturation := 0;
            des_a > 3 -> (des_a := 3; saturation := 1);
            des_a < -3 -> (des_a := -3; saturation := 1);

            if obs_pos > 0 && veh_pos < obs_pos && obs_pos < veh_pos + safe_d then
                emerg_a := veh_v * veh_v / 2 / (veh_pos - obs_pos);
                cmd := min(emerg_a, des_a)
            else
                cmd := des_a
            endif;
            
            got_result := 1
        $
        busy_comp_acc_imp? --> state := "ready"
        )
    );
    got_result == 1 ->
    (
        <t_dot = 1, exe_time_dot = 1 & exe_time < 0.001 && t < 0.005> |> [] (busy_comp_acc_imp? --> state := "ready");
        if t == 0.005 then
            free!"comp_acc_imp"; state := "inactive"
        elif exe_time >= 0.001 then
            tran_cmd!cmd; free!"comp_acc_imp"; state := "inactive"
        else  # t < 0.005 & exe_time < 0.001
            skip
        endif
    )
endif
)**

COM_velo_voter_imp ::=
state := "inactive"; prior := 1;
(
if state == "inactive" then
    act_velo_voter_imp?;
    t := 0; got_result := 0; state := "ready"
elif state == "ready" then
    ready_velo_voter_imp!prior;
    <t_dot = 1 & t < 0.008> |> [] (run_velo_voter_imp? --> state := "running");
    t == 0.008 -> (free!"velo_voter_imp"; state := "inactive")
else  # state == "running"
    got_result == 0 ->
    (
        exe_time := 0;
        (
        tran_wheel_v2?wheel_v -->
            tran_wheel_valid2?wheel_valid;
            tran_laser_v2?laser_v;
            tran_laser_valid2?laser_valid;
            if wheel_valid < 0 then
                veh_v := laser_v
            elif laser_valid < 0 then
                veh_v := wheel_v
            else
                veh_v := (wheel_v + laser_v) / 2
            endif;
            got_result := 1
        $
        busy_velo_voter_imp? -->
            state := "ready"
        )
    );
    got_result == 1 ->
    (
        <t_dot = 1, exe_time_dot = 1 & exe_time< 0.001 && t < 0.008> |> [] (busy_velo_voter_imp? --> state := "ready");
        if t == 0.008 then
            free!"velo_voter_imp"; state := "inactive"
        elif exe_time >= 0.001 then
            tran_veh_v!veh_v; free!"velo_voter_imp"; state := "inactive"
        else  # t < 0.008 & exe_time < 0.001
            skip
        endif
    )
endif

COM_pan_ctr_th_imp ::=
des_v := 0;
state := "inactive"; prior := 0;
(
if state == "inactive" then
    (act_pan_ctr_th_imp_inc? --> skip $ act_pan_ctr_th_imp_dec? --> skip);
    t := 0; got_result := 0; state := "ready"
elif state == "ready" then
    ready_pan_ctr_th_imp!prior;
    <t_dot = 1 & t < 0.1> |> [] (run_pan_ctr_th_imp? --> state := "running");
    t == 0.1 -> (free!"pan_ctr_th_imp"; state := "inactive")
else  # state == "running"
    got_result == 0 ->
    (
        exe_time := 0;
        (
        inc?event --> des_v := des_v + 1; got_result := 1
        $
        dec?event --> des_v := des_v - 1; got_result := 1
        $
        busy_pan_ctr_th_imp? --> state := "ready"
        )
    );
    got_result == 1 ->
    (
        <t_dot = 1, exe_time_dot = 1 & exe_time < 0.001 && t < 0.1> |> [] (busy_pan_ctr_th_imp? --> state := "ready");
        if t == 0.1 then
            free!"pan_ctr_th_imp"; state := "inactive"
        elif exe_time >= 0.001 then
            tran_des_v!des_v; free!"pan_ctr_th_imp"; state := "inactive"
        else  # t < 0.1 & exe_time < 0.001
            skip
        endif
    )
endif
)**

inc_get!"inc"; inc_get!"inc"; inc_get!"inc"; inc_get!"inc"; wait(4); dec_get!"dec"; dec_get!"dec"

vehicle_imp ::=
v := 0; s := 0; min_v := -10; max_v := 10;
sent_veh_l_v := 0; sent_veh_w_v := 0; sent_veh_s := 0;
(
tran_veh_l_v!v --> sent_veh_l_v := 1
$
tran_veh_w_v!v --> sent_veh_w_v := 1
$
tran_veh_s!s --> sent_veh_s := 1
){sent_veh_l_v == 0 || sent_veh_w_v == 0 || sent_veh_s == 0}**;
tran_veh_a?a;
(
v <= min_v ->
    <s_dot = min_v, v_dot = a & v <= min_v> |> []
    (tran_veh_l_v!min_v --> skip, tran_veh_w_v!min_v --> skip, tran_veh_s!s --> skip, tran_veh_a?a --> skip);
min_v < v && v < max_v ->
    <s_dot = v, v_dot = a & true> |> []
    (tran_veh_l_v!v --> skip, tran_veh_w_v!v --> skip, tran_veh_s!s --> skip, tran_veh_a?a --> skip);
v >= max_v ->
    <s_dot = max_v, v_dot = a & v >= max_v> |> []
    (tran_veh_l_v!max_v --> skip, tran_veh_w_v!max_v --> skip, tran_veh_s!s --> skip, tran_veh_a?a --> skip)
)**

# buffer on inc event port
inc_buffer ::=
buffer := [];
(
if len(buffer) == 0 then
    inc_get1?event; buffer := push(buffer, event)
else  # len(buffer) > 0
    inc_get1?event --> buffer := push(buffer, event)
    $
    inc!bottom(buffer) --> buffer := get(buffer)
    $
    act_pan_ctr_th_imp_inc! --> skip
endif
)**

# buffer on dec event port
dec_buffer ::=
buffer := [];
(
if len(buffer) == 0 then
    dec_get1?event; buffer := push(buffer, event)
else  # len(buffer) > 0
    dec_get1?event --> buffer := push(buffer, event)
    $
    dec!bottom(buffer) --> buffer := get(buffer)
    $
    act_pan_ctr_th_imp_dec! --> skip
endif
)**
